NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE

[Part VI—Sec. 4

PUBLIC NOTICE
FORM No.155
[See Rule 329]
Members Winding Up
Name of the Company: NATURE REMEDIES PRIVATE LIMITED
Notice Convening Final Meeting

Notice is hereby given in pursuance of Section 497 of the Companies Act, 1956, that a General Meeting of the
Members of the above named Company will be held on Wednesday 21st day of January 2015, at 75/47 Fourth Avenue,
Ashok Nagar, Chennai-600 083 at 11.00 A.M., for the purpose of having an account laid before the members showing them
the manner in which the winding up has been conducted and the property of the company disposed off and of hearing any
explanation that may be given by the liquidator and also of determining by special resolution of the company, the manner
in which the books, accounts and documents of the company and of the liquidator shall be disposed off.

Chennai,

R. ALAGAR.

3rd December 2014.

Liquidator.

PRINTED AND PUBLISHED BY THE DIRECTOR OF STATIONERY AND PRINTING, CHENNAI
ON BEHALF OF THE GOVERNMENT OF TAMIL NADU
